# Enhanced Spam Lists - GoldRush API Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://goldrush.dev/docs/resources/enhanced-spam-lists#content-area)

[GoldRush API Documentation home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/goldrush/6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA&q=85&s=97917fde1507b0c14e79b83959fe1160)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/goldrush/6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA&q=85&s=5bd4f921dcc81186bf369e7b33ec5734)](https://goldrush.dev/docs)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Resources

Enhanced Spam Lists

[Overview](https://goldrush.dev/docs/overview)
[Foundational API](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api/overview)
[Streaming API](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/overview)
[Chains](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/overview)

On this page

*   [Step 1. Install the Package](https://goldrush.dev/docs/resources/enhanced-spam-lists#step-1-install-the-package)
    
*   [Step 2. Use Cases](https://goldrush.dev/docs/resources/enhanced-spam-lists#step-2-use-cases)
    

The GoldRush Enhanced Spam Lists are a public good designed to restore trust and transparency in the Web3 ecosystem by helping developers, explorers, wallets, and indexers protect their users from scam tokens and malicious contracts. The Enhanced Spam Lists can be accessed as an [npm package](https://www.npmjs.com/package/@covalenthq/goldrush-enhanced-spam-lists)
.

This package requires Node.js v18 or above.

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/resources/enhanced-spam-lists#step-1-install-the-package)

Step 1. Install the Package

You can install the package using npm, yarn or pnpm:

npm

yarn

pnpm

Copy

Ask AI

    npm install @covalenthq/goldrush-enhanced-spam-lists
    

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/resources/enhanced-spam-lists#step-2-use-cases)

Step 2. Use Cases

1

Verify if an ERC20 token is spam on a given network

Copy

Ask AI

    import {
        Networks,
        isERC20Spam,
    } from "@covalenthq/goldrush-enhanced-spam-lists";
    
    // With default options
    const isSpam = await isERC20Spam("0xTokenAddress", Networks.ETHEREUM_MAINNET);
    console.log(isSpam);
    

2

For a potential spam check for an ERC20 token, Confidence.MAYBE can be used

Copy

Ask AI

    import {
        Confidence,
        Networks,
        isERC20Spam,
    } from "@covalenthq/goldrush-enhanced-spam-lists";
    
    const isPotentialSpam = await isERC20Spam(
        "0xTokenAddress",
        Networks.POLYGON_MAINNET,
        Confidence.MAYBE
    );
    console.log(isPotentialSpam);
    

3

Verify if an NFT token is spam on a given network

Copy

Ask AI

    import {
            Networks,
            isNFTSpam,
    } from "@covalenthq/goldrush-enhanced-spam-lists";
    
    const isNftSpam = await isNFTSpam("0xNftAddress", Networks.BSC_MAINNET);
    console.log(isNftSpam);
    

4

Control caching behavior

Copy

Ask AI

    import {
        Networks,
        Confidence,
        isERC20Spam,
        clearCache,
    } from "@covalenthq/goldrush-enhanced-spam-lists";
    
    // With caching enabled (default)
    const withCache = await isERC20Spam(
        "0xTokenAddress",
        Networks.ETHEREUM_MAINNET,
        Confidence.YES,
        true // Enable caching (default)
    );
    
    // Without caching (always fetches fresh data)
    const withoutCache = await isERC20Spam(
        "0xTokenAddress",
        Networks.ETHEREUM_MAINNET,
        Confidence.YES,
        false // Disable caching
    );
    
    // Clear memory and disk cache if needed
    clearCache();
    

5

For more control, you can get the full lists:

Copy

Ask AI

    import {
        getERC20List,
        getNFTList,
        Confidence,
        Networks,
    } from "@covalenthq/goldrush-enhanced-spam-lists";
    
    // Get ERC20 spam list with default caching
    const ethSpamTokens = await getERC20List(Networks.ETHEREUM_MAINNET, Confidence.YES);
    
    // Get NFT spam list with caching disabled
    const bscSpamNfts = await getNFTList(Networks.BSC_MAINNET, false);
    

6

Get the specific spam score for a given contract

Copy

Ask AI

    import {
        getERC20List,
        getSpamScore,
        Networks,
        Confidence,
    } from "@covalenthq/goldrush-enhanced-spam-lists";
    
    const ethSpamTokens = await getERC20List(
    Networks.ETHEREUM_MAINNET,
    Confidence.YES
    );
    const score = getSpamScore(ethSpamTokens[0]);
    console.log(score); // Returns the spam score as a string

GoldRush SDK

TypeScript

Copy

Ask AI

    import { GoldRushClient } from "@covalenthq/client-sdk";
    
    const ApiServices = async () => {
        const client = new GoldRushClient("YOUR_API_KEY");
        const resp = await client.BalanceService.getErc20TransfersForWalletAddress({chainName: "chainName", walletAddress: "walletAddress"});
        console.log(resp.data);
    };
    
    ApiServices();

Credit Cost
-----------

0.05 per item

Processing
----------

Realtime

Related guides

[Understanding Web3 Wallets with GoldRush](https://goldrush.dev/guides/understanding-web3-wallets)
[Calculate Crypto Cost Basis and Capital Gains with GoldRush](https://goldrush.dev/guides/calculate-crypto-cost-basis-and-capital-gains-with-covalent)
[DIY - Build Your Own Crypto Tax Calculator with Google Sheets](https://goldrush.dev/guides/diy-build-your-own-crypto-tax-calculator-with-google-sheets)
[How to Use Covalent’s Wallet Transaction Analysis Tool](https://goldrush.dev/guides/how-to-use-covalent-s-wallet-transaction-analysis-tool)

#### Authorizations

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-erc20-token-transfers-for-address#authorization-authorization)

Authorization

string

header

required

Bearer authentication header of the form: `Bearer <token>`, where `<token>` is your GoldRush API Key.

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-erc20-token-transfers-for-address#parameter-chain-name)

chainName

string

required

The chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-erc20-token-transfers-for-address#parameter-wallet-address)

walletAddress

string

required

The requested address. Passing in an `ENS`, `RNS`, `Lens Handle`, or an `Unstoppable Domain` resolves automatically.

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-erc20-token-transfers-for-address#parameter-quote-currency)

quote-currency

string

The currency to convert. Supports `USD`, `CAD`, `EUR`, `SGD`, `INR`, `JPY`, `VND`, `CNY`, `KRW`, `RUB`, `TRY`, `NGN`, `ARS`, `AUD`, `CHF`, and `GBP`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-erc20-token-transfers-for-address#parameter-contract-address)

contract-address

string

required

The requested contract address. Passing in an `ENS`, `RNS`, `Lens Handle`, or an `Unstoppable Domain` resolves automatically.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-erc20-token-transfers-for-address#parameter-starting-block)

starting-block

integer

The block height to start from, defaults to `0`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-erc20-token-transfers-for-address#parameter-ending-block)

ending-block

integer

The block height to end at, defaults to current block height.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-erc20-token-transfers-for-address#parameter-page-size)

page-size

integer

Number of items per page. Omitting this parameter defaults to 100.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-erc20-token-transfers-for-address#parameter-page-number)

page-number

integer

0-indexed page number to begin pagination.

#### Response

200 - application/json

Successful response

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-erc20-token-transfers-for-address#response-address)

address

string

The requested address.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-erc20-token-transfers-for-address#response-updated-at)

updated\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp when the response was generated. Useful to show data staleness to users.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-erc20-token-transfers-for-address#response-quote-currency)

quote\_currency

string

The requested quote currency eg: `USD`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-erc20-token-transfers-for-address#response-chain-id)

chain\_id

integer

The requested chain ID eg: `1`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-erc20-token-transfers-for-address#response-chain-name)

chain\_name

string

The requested chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-erc20-token-transfers-for-address#response-chain-tip-height)

chain\_tip\_height

integer

The latest block height of the blockchain at the time this response was provided.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-erc20-token-transfers-for-address#response-chain-tip-signed-at)

chain\_tip\_signed\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp of the latest signed block at the time this response was provided.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-erc20-token-transfers-for-address#response-items)

items

object\[\]

List of response items.

Show child attributes

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-erc20-token-transfers-for-address#response-pagination)

pagination

object

Pagination metadata.

Show child attributes

[Get historical portfolio value over time](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-portfolio-value-over-time)

Get Bitcoin balance for non-HD address

[Overview](https://goldrush.dev/docs/overview)
[Foundational API](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api/overview)
[Streaming API](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/overview)

GoldRush SDK

TypeScript

Copy

Ask AI

    import { GoldRushClient } from "@covalenthq/client-sdk";
    
    const ApiServices = async () => {
        const client = new GoldRushClient("YOUR_API_KEY");
        const resp = await client.BalanceService.getBitcoinBalanceForWalletAddress({chainName: "chainName", walletAddress: "walletAddress"});
        console.log(resp.data);
    };
    
    ApiServices();

          "block_height": 123,\
          "native_token": true,\
          "type": "<string>",\
          "is_spam": true,\
          "balance": "<string>",\
          "balance_24h": "<string>",\
          "quote_rate": 123,\
          "quote_rate_24h": 123,\
          "quote": 123,\
          "quote_24h": 123,\
          "pretty_quote": "<string>",\
          "pretty_quote_24h": "<string>",\
          "protocol_metadata": {\
            "protocol_name": "<string>"\
          }\
        }\
      ]
    }

GET

/

v1

/

btc-mainnet

/

address

/

{walletAddress}

/

balances\_v2

Try it

GoldRush SDK

TypeScript

Copy

Ask AI

    import { GoldRushClient } from "@covalenthq/client-sdk";
    
    const ApiServices = async () => {
        const client = new GoldRushClient("YOUR_API_KEY");
        const resp = await client.BalanceService.getBitcoinBalanceForWalletAddress({chainName: "chainName", walletAddress: "walletAddress"});
        console.log(resp.data);
    };
    
    ApiServices();

200

Credit Cost
-----------

1 per call

Processing
----------

Realtime

#### Authorizations

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-bitcoin-balance-for-address#authorization-authorization)

Authorization

string

header

required

Bearer authentication header of the form: `Bearer <token>`, where `<token>` is your GoldRush API Key.

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-bitcoin-balance-for-address#parameter-wallet-address)

walletAddress

string

required

The requested bitcoin non-HD address.

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-bitcoin-balance-for-address#parameter-quote-currency)

quote-currency

string

The currency to convert. Supports `USD`, `CAD`, `EUR`, `SGD`, `INR`, `JPY`, `VND`, `CNY`, `KRW`, `RUB`, `TRY`, `NGN`, `ARS`, `AUD`, `CHF`, and `GBP`.

#### Response

200 - application/json

Successful response

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-bitcoin-balance-for-address#response-address)

address

string

The requested address.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-bitcoin-balance-for-address#response-chain-id)

chain\_id

integer

The requested chain ID eg: `1`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-bitcoin-balance-for-address#response-chain-name)

chain\_name

string

The requested chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-bitcoin-balance-for-address#response-chain-tip-height)

chain\_tip\_height

integer

The latest block height of the blockchain at the time this response was provided.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-bitcoin-balance-for-address#response-chain-tip-signed-at)

chain\_tip\_signed\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp of the latest signed block at the time this response was provided.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-bitcoin-balance-for-address#response-quote-currency)

quote\_currency

string

The requested quote currency eg: `USD`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-bitcoin-balance-for-address#response-updated-at)

updated\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp when the response was generated. Useful to show data staleness to users.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-bitcoin-balance-for-address#response-items)

items

object\[\]

List of response items.

Show child attributes

[Get Bitcoin balances for HD address](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-bitcoin-balances-for-hd-address)
[Get historical Bitcoin balance for non-HD address](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-bitcoin-balance-for-address)

⌘I

GoldRush SDK

TypeScript

Copy

Ask AI

    import { GoldRushClient } from "@covalenthq/client-sdk";
    
    const ApiServices = async () => {
        const client = new GoldRushClient("YOUR_API_KEY");
        const resp = await client.NftService.checkOwnershipInNft({chainName: "chainName", walletAddress: "walletAddress"});
        console.log(resp.data);
    };
    
    ApiServices();

Credit Cost
-----------

1 per call

Processing
----------

Batch

Related guides

[How to Block NFT Spam](https://goldrush.dev/guides/how-to-block-spam-nft-tokens)
[Mastering the ERC-1155 Multi-Token Standard (Part 2)](https://goldrush.dev/guides/mastering-the-erc-1155-multi-token-standard-part-2)
[How to Verify NFT Ownership in a Collection](https://goldrush.dev/guides/how-to-verify-nft-ownership-in-a-collection)
[How to Create an NFT Allowlist (AKA Whitelist)](https://goldrush.dev/guides/how-to-create-an-nft-allowlist)
[How Token Gating and Membership dApps Use the GoldRush API](https://goldrush.dev/guides/how-token-gating-dapps-use-the-covalent-api)

#### Authorizations

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/nft/check-ownership-in-nft-collection#authorization-authorization)

Authorization

string

header

required

Bearer authentication header of the form: `Bearer <token>`, where `<token>` is your GoldRush API Key.

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/nft/check-ownership-in-nft-collection#parameter-chain-name)

chainName

string

required

The chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/nft/check-ownership-in-nft-collection#parameter-wallet-address)

walletAddress

string

required

The requested address. Passing in an `ENS`, `RNS`, `Lens Handle`, or an `Unstoppable Domain` resolves automatically.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/nft/check-ownership-in-nft-collection#parameter-collection-contract)

collectionContract

string

required

The requested collection address.

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/nft/check-ownership-in-nft-collection#parameter-traits-filter)

traits-filter

string

Filters NFTs based on a specific trait. If this filter is used, the API will return all NFTs with the specified trait. Must be used with "values-filter", is case-sensitive, and requires proper URL encoding.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/nft/check-ownership-in-nft-collection#parameter-values-filter)

values-filter

string

Filters NFTs based on a specific trait value. If this filter is used, the API will return all NFTs with the specified trait value. Must be used with "traits-filter", is case-sensitive, and requires proper URL encoding.

#### Response

200 - application/json

Successful response

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/nft/check-ownership-in-nft-collection#response-updated-at)

updated\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp when the response was generated. Useful to show data staleness to users.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/nft/check-ownership-in-nft-collection#response-address)

address

string

The requested address.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/nft/check-ownership-in-nft-collection#response-collection)

collection

string

The requested collection.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/nft/check-ownership-in-nft-collection#response-is-spam)

is\_spam

boolean

Denotes whether the token is suspected spam. Supported on all Foundational Chains.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/nft/check-ownership-in-nft-collection#response-items)

items

object\[\]

List of response items.

Show child attributes

[Get NFTs for address](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/nft/get-nfts-for-address)
[Check ownership in NFT collection for specific token](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/nft/check-ownership-in-nft-collection-token)

Credit Cost
-----------

1 per call

Processing
----------

Batch

Supports pools on Uniswap V2, V3 and their forks on all [Foundational Chains](https://goldrush.dev/chains/)
.

#### Authorizations

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-pool-spot-prices#authorization-authorization)

Authorization

string

header

required

Bearer authentication header of the form: `Bearer <token>`, where `<token>` is your GoldRush API Key.

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-pool-spot-prices#parameter-chain-name)

chainName

string

required

The chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-pool-spot-prices#parameter-contract-address)

contractAddress

string

required

The pool contract address.

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-pool-spot-prices#parameter-quote-currency)

quote-currency

string

The currency to convert. Supports `USD`, `CAD`, `EUR`, `SGD`, `INR`, `JPY`, `VND`, `CNY`, `KRW`, `RUB`, `TRY`, `NGN`, `ARS`, `AUD`, `CHF`, and `GBP`.

#### Response

200 - application/json

Successful response

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-pool-spot-prices#response-updated-at)

updated\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp when the response was generated.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-pool-spot-prices#response-pool-address)

pool\_address

string

The deployed pool contract address.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-pool-spot-prices#response-token-0-address)

token\_0\_address

string

The deployed contract address of `token_0` in the token pair making up the pool.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-pool-spot-prices#response-token-0-name)

token\_0\_name

string

The deployed contract name of `token_0` in the token pair making up the pool.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-pool-spot-prices#response-token-0-ticker)

token\_0\_ticker

string

The deployed contract symbol of `token_0` in the token pair making up the pool.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-pool-spot-prices#response-token-0-price)

token\_0\_price

string

Price of `token_0` in units of `token_1`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-pool-spot-prices#response-token-0-price-24h)

token\_0\_price\_24h

string

Price of `token_0` in units of `token_1` as of 24 hours ago.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-pool-spot-prices#response-token-0-price-quote)

token\_0\_price\_quote

string

Price of `token_0` in the selected quote currency (defaults to USD).

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-pool-spot-prices#response-token-0-price-24h-quote)

token\_0\_price\_24h\_quote

string

Price of `token_0` in the selected quote currency (defaults to USD) as of 24 hours ago.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-pool-spot-prices#response-token-1-address)

token\_1\_address

string

The deployed contract address of `token_1` in the token pair making up the pool.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-pool-spot-prices#response-token-1-name)

token\_1\_name

string

The deployed contract name of `token_1` in the token pair making up the pool.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-pool-spot-prices#response-token-1-ticker)

token\_1\_ticker

string

The deployed contract symbol of `token_1` in the token pair making up the pool.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-pool-spot-prices#response-token-1-price)

token\_1\_price

string

Price of `token_1` in units of `token_0`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-pool-spot-prices#response-token-1-price-24h)

token\_1\_price\_24h

string

Price of `token_1` in units of `token_0` as of 24 hours ago.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-pool-spot-prices#response-token-1-price-quote)

token\_1\_price\_quote

string

Price of `token_1` in the selected quote currency (defaults to USD).

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-pool-spot-prices#response-token-1-price-24h-quote)

token\_1\_price\_24h\_quote

string

Price of `token_1` in the selected quote currency (defaults to USD) as of 24 hours ago.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-pool-spot-prices#response-quote-currency)

quote\_currency

string

The currency to convert. Supports `USD`, `CAD`, `EUR`, `SGD`, `INR`, `JPY`, `VND`, `CNY`, `KRW`, `RUB`, `TRY`, `NGN`, `ARS`, `AUD`, `CHF`, `GBP`, `BTC` and `ETH`.

Resources

Decoded Events

[Overview](https://goldrush.dev/docs/overview)
[Foundational API](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api/overview)
[Streaming API](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/overview)
[Chains](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/overview)

On this page

*   [Transfer Event](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/decoded-events#transfer-event)
    
*   [Swap Event](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/decoded-events#swap-event)
    
*   [Bridge Event](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/decoded-events#bridge-event)
    
*   [Deposit Event](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/decoded-events#deposit-event)

*   [Error Details](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/decoded-events#error-details)
    

The following events are decoded in the GoldRush Streaming API:

*   [Transfer](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/decoded-events#transfer-event)
    
*   [Swap](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/decoded-events#swap-event)
    
*   [Bridge](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/decoded-events#bridge-event)
    
*   [Deposit](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/decoded-events#deposit-event)
    
*   [Withdraw](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/decoded-events#withdraw-event)
    
*   [Approve](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/decoded-events#approve-event)
    

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/decoded-events#transfer-event)

Transfer Event
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `from` | `string` | The source address |
| `to` | `string` | The destination address |
| `amount` | `string` | Unscaled token amount (scale by `metadata.contract_decimals`) |
| `quote_rate_usd` | `string` | Exchange rate of the token in USD |
| `quote_usd` | `string` | The quote amount of the token in USD |
| `contract_metadata` | `object` | Contract details including `contract_name`, `contract_address`, `contract_decimals`, and `contract_ticker_symbol` |

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/decoded-events#swap-event)

Swap Event
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `token_in` | `string` | The input token address |
| `token_out` | `string` | The output token address |
| `amount_in` | `string` | The amount of input tokens |
| `amount_out` | `string` | The amount of output tokens |

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/decoded-events#bridge-event)

Bridge Event
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `type` | `string` | The bridge transaction type |
| `typeString` | `string` | Human-readable bridge transaction type |
| `from` | `string` | The source address |
| `to` | `string` | The destination address |
| `amount` | `string` | Unscaled token amount (scale by `metadata.contract_decimals`) |
| `quote_rate_usd` | `string` | Exchange rate of the token in USD |
| `quote_usd` | `string` | The quote amount of the token in USD |
| `contract_metadata` | `object` | Contract details including `contract_name`, `contract_address`, `contract_decimals`, and `contract_ticker_symbol` |

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/decoded-events#deposit-event)

Deposit Event
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `from` | `string` | The source address |
| `to` | `string` | The destination address |
| `amount` | `string` | Unscaled token amount (scale by `metadata.contract_decimals`) |
| `quote_rate_usd` | `string` | Exchange rate of the token in USD |
| `quote_usd` | `string` | The quote amount of the token in USD |
| `contract_metadata` | `object` | Contract details including `contract_name`, `contract_address`, `contract_decimals`, and `contract_ticker_symbol` |

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/decoded-events#withdraw-event)

Withdraw Event
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `from` | `string` | The source address |
| `to` | `string` | The destination address |
| `amount` | `string` | Unscaled token amount (scale by `metadata.contract_decimals`) |
| `quote_rate_usd` | `string` | Exchange rate of the token in USD |
| `quote_usd` | `string` | The quote amount of the token in USD |
| `contract_metadata` | `object` | Contract details including `contract_name`, `contract_address`, `contract_decimals`, and `contract_ticker_symbol` |

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/decoded-events#approve-event)

Approve Event
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `spender` | `string` | The address approved to spend tokens |
| `amount` | `string` | Unscaled token amount (scale by `metadata.contract_decimals`) |
| `quote_rate_usd` | `string` | Exchange rate of the token in USD |
| `quote_usd` | `string` | The quote amount of the token in USD |
| `contract_metadata` | `object` | Contract details including `contract_name`, `contract_address`, `contract_decimals`, and `contract_ticker_symbol` |

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/decoded-events#transaction-logs)

Transaction Logs
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `emitter_address` | `string` | The address that emitted the log |
| `log_offset` | `integer` | The offset of the log in the transaction |
| `data` | `string` | The raw log data |
| `topics` | `array` | Array of log topics |

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/decoded-events#error-details)

Error Details
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `message` | `string` | Error message describing what went wrong |

[GraphQL Endpoints](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/graphql-endpoints)
[GoldRush Playground](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-playground)

# Check ownership in NFT collection for specific token - GoldRush API Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/nft/check-ownership-in-nft-collection-token#content-area)

NFT

Check ownership in NFT collection for specific token

[Overview](https://goldrush.dev/docs/overview)
[Foundational API](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api/overview)
[Streaming API](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/overview)
[Chains](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/overview)

GoldRush SDK

TypeScript

Copy

Ask AI

    import { GoldRushClient } from "@covalenthq/client-sdk";
    
    const ApiServices = async () => {
        const client = new GoldRushClient("YOUR_API_KEY");
        const resp = await client.NftService.checkOwnershipInNftForSpecificTokenId({chainName: "chainName", walletAddress: "walletAddress"});
        console.log(resp.data);
    };
    
    ApiServices();

Credit Cost
-----------

1 per call

Processing
----------

Batch

Related guides

[How to Block NFT Spam](https://goldrush.dev/guides/how-to-block-spam-nft-tokens)
[How to Verify NFT Ownership in a Collection](https://goldrush.dev/guides/how-to-verify-nft-ownership-in-a-collection)
[How to Create an NFT Allowlist (AKA Whitelist)](https://goldrush.dev/guides/how-to-create-an-nft-allowlist)
[How Token Gating and Membership dApps Use the GoldRush API](https://goldrush.dev/guides/how-token-gating-dapps-use-the-covalent-api)

#### Authorizations

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/nft/check-ownership-in-nft-collection-token#authorization-authorization)

Authorization

string

header

required

Bearer authentication header of the form: `Bearer <token>`, where `<token>` is your GoldRush API Key.

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/nft/check-ownership-in-nft-collection-token#parameter-chain-name)

chainName

string

required

The chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/nft/check-ownership-in-nft-collection-token#parameter-wallet-address)

walletAddress

string

required

The requested address. Passing in an `ENS`, `RNS`, `Lens Handle`, or an `Unstoppable Domain` resolves automatically.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/nft/check-ownership-in-nft-collection-token#parameter-collection-contract)

collectionContract

string

required

The requested collection address. Passing in an `ENS`, `RNS`, `Lens Handle`, or an `Unstoppable Domain` resolves automatically.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/nft/check-ownership-in-nft-collection-token#parameter-token-id)

tokenId

string

required

The requested token ID.

#### Response

200 - application/json

Successful response

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/nft/check-ownership-in-nft-collection-token#response-updated-at)

updated\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp when the response was generated. Useful to show data staleness to users.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/nft/check-ownership-in-nft-collection-token#response-address)

address

string

The requested address.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/nft/check-ownership-in-nft-collection-token#response-collection)

collection

string

The requested collection.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/nft/check-ownership-in-nft-collection-token#response-is-spam)

is\_spam

boolean

Denotes whether the token is suspected spam. Supported on all Foundational Chains.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/nft/check-ownership-in-nft-collection-token#response-items)

items

object\[\]

List of response items.

Show child attributes

[Check ownership in NFT collection](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/nft/check-ownership-in-nft-collection)
[Get token approvals for address](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/security/get-token-approvals-for-address)

    import { GoldRushClient } from "@covalenthq/client-sdk";
    
    const ApiServices = async () => {
        const client = new GoldRushClient("YOUR_API_KEY");
        const resp = await client.BaseService.getGasPrices({chainName: "chainName", walletAddress: "walletAddress"});
        console.log(resp.data);
    };
    
    ApiServices();

Credit Cost
-----------

1 per call

Processing
----------

Batch

Currently support these event types: `erc20` token transfers, `nativetokens` transfer, and `uniswapv3` swap events.

Related guides

[How to Fetch Onchain Gas Prices and Estimate Gas Costs](https://goldrush.dev/guides/how-to-fetch-gas-prices-and-estimate-gas-costs)

#### Authorizations

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-gas-prices#authorization-authorization)

Authorization

string

header

required

Bearer authentication header of the form: `Bearer <token>`, where `<token>` is your GoldRush API Key.

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-gas-prices#parameter-chain-name)

chainName

string

required

The chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-gas-prices#parameter-event-type)

eventType

string

required

The desired event type to retrieve gas prices for. Supports `erc20` transfer events, `uniswapv3` swap events and `nativetokens` transfers.

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-gas-prices#parameter-quote-currency)

quote-currency

string

The currency to convert. Supports `USD`, `CAD`, `EUR`, `SGD`, `INR`, `JPY`, `VND`, `CNY`, `KRW`, `RUB`, `TRY`, `NGN`, `ARS`, `AUD`, `CHF`, and `GBP`.

#### Response

200 - application/json

Successful response

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-gas-prices#response-chain-id)

chain\_id

integer

The requested chain ID eg: `1`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-gas-prices#response-chain-name)

chain\_name

string

The requested chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-gas-prices#response-quote-currency)

quote\_currency

string

The requested quote currency eg: `USD`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-gas-prices#response-updated-at)

updated\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp when the response was generated. Useful to show data staleness to users.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-gas-prices#response-event-type)

event\_type

string

The requested event type.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-gas-prices#response-gas-quote-rate)

gas\_quote\_rate

number<double>

The exchange rate for the requested quote currency.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-gas-prices#response-base-fee)

base\_fee

string

b;The lowest gas fee for the latest block height.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-gas-prices#response-items)

items

object\[\]

List of response items.

Show child attributes

[Get pool spot prices](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-pool-spot-prices)
[Get logs](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-logs)

#### Authorizations

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-a-block#authorization-authorization)

Authorization

string

header

required

Bearer authentication header of the form: `Bearer <token>`, where `<token>` is your GoldRush API Key.

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-a-block#parameter-chain-name)

chainName

string

required

The chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-a-block#parameter-block-height)

blockHeight

string

required

The block height or `latest` for the latest block available.

#### Response

200 - application/json

Successful response

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-a-block#response-updated-at)

updated\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp when the response was generated. Useful to show data staleness to users.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-a-block#response-chain-id)

chain\_id

integer

The requested chain ID eg: `1`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-a-block#response-chain-name)

chain\_name

string

The requested chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-a-block#response-items)

items

object\[\]

List of response items.

# Get PnL for wallet - GoldRush API Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-wallet#content-area)

[GoldRush API Documentation home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/goldrush/6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA&q=85&s=97917fde1507b0c14e79b83959fe1160)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/goldrush/6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA&q=85&s=5bd4f921dcc81186bf369e7b33ec5734)](https://goldrush.dev/docs)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Available Queries

Get PnL for wallet

[Overview](https://goldrush.dev/docs/overview)
[Foundational API](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api/overview)
[Streaming API](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/overview)
[Chains](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/overview)

On this page

*   [Parameters](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-wallet#parameters)
    
*   [Query](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-wallet#query)
    
*   [Basic Query](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-wallet#basic-query)
    
*   [Complete Query](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-wallet#complete-query)
    
*   [Response Format](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-wallet#response-format)
    
*   [Field Descriptions](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-wallet#field-descriptions)
    
*   [GraphQL Playground](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-wallet#graphql-playground)
    

This GraphQL query provides detailed financial metrics, including unrealized and realized profit and loss (PnL), current balance, and transaction insights for each token held by a specific wallet address.

Credit Cost
-----------

TBD

Supported Chains
----------------

*   Base Mainnet
*   BSC Mainnet
*   Ethereum Mainnet
*   Gnosis Mainnet
*   Polygon Mainnet
*   Optimism Mainnet

**This query is currently in Beta.** It is stable for testing and evaluation but may undergo changes in schema or behavior as we continue to improve it. **No API credits are currently charged.**We welcome your feedback so please [reach out](https://goldrush.dev/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#e3909693938c9197a3808c95828f868d978b92cd808c8e)
 to us directly to report issues or request features.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-wallet#parameters)

Parameters
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Required | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `chain_name` | `enum` | Yes | Chain name to filter events (e.g., `BASE_MAINNET`, `ETH_MAINNET`, `BSC_MAINNET`) |
| `wallet_address` | `string` | Yes | The wallet address to query |

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-wallet#query)

Query
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can query the `upnlForWallet` endpoint to retrieve detailed PnL metrics for a wallet.

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-wallet#basic-query)

Basic Query

Copy

Ask AI

    query {
     upnlForToken(
        chain_name: ETH_MAINNET
        wallet_address: "0xfe97b0C517a84F98fc6eDe3CD26B43012d31992a"
      ) {
        token
        cost_basis
        current_price
        pnl_realized_usd
        pnl_unrealized_usd
        net_balance_change
      }
    }
    
    

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-wallet#complete-query)

Complete Query

Copy

Ask AI

    query{ 
    upnlForWallet(
        chain_name:ETH_MAINNET,
        wallet_address:"0xfe97b0C517a84F98fc6eDe3CD26B43012d31992a"
      ) {
        token
        cost_basis
        current_price
        pnl_realized_usd
        pnl_unrealized_usd
        net_balance_change
        marketcap_usd
        contract_metadata {
          contract_address
          contract_name
          contract_ticker_symbol
          contract_decimals
        }
      }
    }
    

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-wallet#response-format)

Response Format
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Here’s an example of the response data structure:

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "data": {
        "upnlForWallet": [\
          {\
            "token": "0x7abc8a5768e6be61a6c693a6e4eacb5b60602c4d",\
            "cost_basis": 0.03219392,\
            "current_price": 0.032418,\
            "pnl_realized_usd": null,\
            "pnl_unrealized_usd": 318.22842,\
            "net_balance_change": 1420158,\
            "marketcap_usd": "32418001.4431",\
            "contract_metadata": {\
              "contract_address": "0x7abc8a5768e6be61a6c693a6e4eacb5b60602c4d",\
              "contract_name": "Covalent X Token",\
              "contract_ticker_symbol": "CXT",\
              "contract_decimals": 18\
            }\
          }\
        ]
      }
    }
    

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-wallet#field-descriptions)

Field Descriptions

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `token` | `string` | Token contract address, represented in uppercase with a 0x prefix |
| `cost_basis` | `float` | Simple Average cost basis per token in USD |
| `current_price` | `float` | Current market price per token in USD |
| `pnl_realized_usd` | `float` | Realized profit or loss in USD from completed trades |
| `pnl_unrealized_usd` | `float` | Current unrealized profit or loss in USD based on the latest price |
| `net_balance_change` | `BigInteger` | Net token movement (inflow minus outflow) over the past 7 days |
| `marketcap_usd` | `string` | Token’s estimated market capitalization in USD |
| `contract_metadata` | `object` | Contains metadata details for the token contract |

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-wallet#graphql-playground)

GraphQL Playground
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[Get top trading wallets for token](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-token)
[GraphQL Endpoints](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/graphql-endpoints)

⌘I

      }
    }

Credit Cost
-----------

0.02 per item

Processing
----------

Realtime

When no `block-height` is specified, the default is to use the latest token holder snapshot which updates every 30 mins.To fetch the current token holders list without using the snapshot, set `no-snapshot=true`.Page size is either `100` (default) or `1000`.Supported only on [Foundational Chains](https://goldrush.dev/chains/)
.

Related guides

[Getting Started with the GoldRush SDK](https://goldrush.dev/guides/getting-started-with-the-covalent-sdk)
[How to Get NFT Owners at a Specific Block Height Using the GoldRush API](https://goldrush.dev/guides/how-to-get-nft-owners-at-a-specific-block-height-using-the-covalent-api)
[How to Get Token Holder Data for ERC-20, ERC-721 and ERC-1155s](https://goldrush.dev/guides/how-to-get-token-holder-data-for-erc-20-erc-721-and-erc-1155s)

#### Authorizations

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-token-holders-as-of-any-block-height-v2#authorization-authorization)

Authorization

string

header

required

Bearer authentication header of the form: `Bearer <token>`, where `<token>` is your GoldRush API Key.

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-token-holders-as-of-any-block-height-v2#parameter-chain-name)

chainName

string

required

The chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-token-holders-as-of-any-block-height-v2#parameter-token-address)

tokenAddress

string

required

The requested address. Passing in an `ENS`, `RNS`, `Lens Handle`, or an `Unstoppable Domain` resolves automatically.

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-token-holders-as-of-any-block-height-v2#parameter-no-snapshot)

no-snapshot

boolean

Defaults to `false`. Set to `true` to bypass last snapshot and get the latest token holders list.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-token-holders-as-of-any-block-height-v2#parameter-block-height)

block-height

integer

Ending block to define a block range. Omitting this parameter defaults to the latest block height.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-token-holders-as-of-any-block-height-v2#parameter-date)

date

string

Ending date to define a block range (YYYY-MM-DD). Omitting this parameter defaults to the current date.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-token-holders-as-of-any-block-height-v2#parameter-page-size)

page-size

integer

Number of items per page. Note: Currently, only values of `100` and `1000` are supported. Omitting this parameter defaults to 100.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-token-holders-as-of-any-block-height-v2#parameter-page-number)

page-number

integer

0-indexed page number to begin pagination.

#### Response

200 - application/json

Successful response

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-token-holders-as-of-any-block-height-v2#response-updated-at)

updated\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp when the response was generated. Useful to show data staleness to users.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-token-holders-as-of-any-block-height-v2#response-chain-id)

chain\_id

integer

The requested chain ID eg: `1`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-token-holders-as-of-any-block-height-v2#response-chain-name)

chain\_name

string

The requested chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-token-holders-as-of-any-block-height-v2#response-chain-tip-height)

chain\_tip\_height

integer

The latest block height of the blockchain at the time this response was provided.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-token-holders-as-of-any-block-height-v2#response-chain-tip-signed-at)

chain\_tip\_signed\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp of the latest signed block at the time this response was provided.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-token-holders-as-of-any-block-height-v2#response-items)

items

object\[\]

List of response items.

Show child attributes

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-token-holders-as-of-any-block-height-v2#response-pagination)

pagination

object

Pagination metadata.

Show child attributes

[Get historical portfolio value over time](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-portfolio-value-over-time)
[Get a transaction](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-a-transaction)

Credit Cost
-----------

1 per call

Processing
----------

Realtime

Supported on all [Foundational Chains](https://goldrush.dev/chains/)
.

#### Authorizations

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-token-balances-for-address#authorization-authorization)

Authorization

string

header

required

Bearer authentication header of the form: `Bearer <token>`, where `<token>` is your GoldRush API Key.

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-token-balances-for-address#parameter-chain-name)

chainName

string

required

The chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-token-balances-for-address#parameter-wallet-address)

walletAddress

string

required

The requested address. Passing in an `ENS`, `RNS`, `Lens Handle`, or an `Unstoppable Domain` resolves automatically.

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-token-balances-for-address#parameter-quote-currency)

quote-currency

string

The currency to convert. Supports `USD`, `CAD`, `EUR`, `SGD`, `INR`, `JPY`, `VND`, `CNY`, `KRW`, `RUB`, `TRY`, `NGN`, `ARS`, `AUD`, `CHF`, and `GBP`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-token-balances-for-address#parameter-no-spam)

no-spam

boolean

If `true`, the suspected spam tokens are removed. Supported on all Foundational Chains.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-token-balances-for-address#parameter-block-height)

block-height

integer

Ending block to define a block range. Omitting this parameter defaults to the latest block height.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-token-balances-for-address#parameter-date)

date

string

Ending date to define a block range (YYYY-MM-DD). Omitting this parameter defaults to the current date.

#### Response

200 - application/json

Successful response

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-token-balances-for-address#response-address)

address

string

The requested address.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-token-balances-for-address#response-updated-at)

updated\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp when the response was generated. Useful to show data staleness to users.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-token-balances-for-address#response-quote-currency)

quote\_currency

string

The requested quote currency eg: `USD`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-token-balances-for-address#response-chain-id)

chain\_id

integer

The requested chain ID eg: `1`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-token-balances-for-address#response-chain-name)

chain\_name

string

The requested chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-token-balances-for-address#response-chain-tip-height)

chain\_tip\_height

integer

The latest block height of the blockchain at the time this response was provided.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-token-balances-for-address#response-chain-tip-signed-at)

chain\_tip\_signed\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp of the latest signed block at the time this response was provided.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-token-balances-for-address#response-items)

items

object\[\]

List of response items.

Show child attributes

[Get token balances for address](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-token-balances-for-address)
[Get native token balance for address](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-native-token-balance)

⌘I

Credit Cost
-----------

0.1 per item

Processing
----------

Realtime

#### Authorizations

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-all-transactions-in-a-block-by-page#authorization-authorization)

Authorization

string

header

required

Bearer authentication header of the form: `Bearer <token>`, where `<token>` is your GoldRush API Key.

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-all-transactions-in-a-block-by-page#parameter-chain-name)

chainName

string

required

The chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-all-transactions-in-a-block-by-page#parameter-block-height)

blockHeight

integer

required

The requested block height. Also accepts `latest` to get latest block.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-all-transactions-in-a-block-by-page#parameter-page)

page

integer

required

The requested 0-indexed page number.

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-all-transactions-in-a-block-by-page#parameter-quote-currency)

quote-currency

string

The currency to convert. Supports `USD`, `CAD`, `EUR`, `SGD`, `INR`, `JPY`, `VND`, `CNY`, `KRW`, `RUB`, `TRY`, `NGN`, `ARS`, `AUD`, `CHF`, and `GBP`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-all-transactions-in-a-block-by-page#parameter-no-logs)

no-logs

boolean

Omit log events.

#### Response

200 - application/json

Successful response

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-all-transactions-in-a-block-by-page#response-updated-at)

updated\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp when the response was generated. Useful to show data staleness to users.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-all-transactions-in-a-block-by-page#response-chain-id)

chain\_id

integer

The requested chain ID eg: `1`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-all-transactions-in-a-block-by-page#response-chain-name)

chain\_name

string

The requested chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-all-transactions-in-a-block-by-page#response-chain-tip-height)

chain\_tip\_height

integer

The latest block height of the blockchain at the time this response was provided.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-all-transactions-in-a-block-by-page#response-chain-tip-signed-at)

chain\_tip\_signed\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp of the latest signed block at the time this response was provided.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-all-transactions-in-a-block-by-page#response-links)

links

object

Show child attributes

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-all-transactions-in-a-block-by-page#response-items)

items

object\[\]

List of response items.

# Get all transactions in a block (v3) - GoldRush API Documentation

Get all transactions in a block (v3)

[Foundational API](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api/overview)
[Streaming API](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/overview)
[Chains](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/overview)

GoldRush SDK

TypeScript

Copy

Ask AI

    import { GoldRushClient } from "@covalenthq/client-sdk";
    
    const ApiServices = async () => {
        const client = new GoldRushClient("YOUR_API_KEY");
        const resp = await client.TransactionService.getTransactionsForBlockHash({chainName: "chainName", walletAddress: "walletAddress"});
        console.log(resp.data);
    };
    
    ApiServices();

    import { GoldRushClient } from "@covalenthq/client-sdk";

        const client = new GoldRushClient("YOUR_API_KEY");
        const resp = await client.TransactionService.getTransactionsForBlockHash({chainName: "chainName", walletAddress: "walletAddress"});

    };

Related guides

[Introducing Transactions V3 APIs](https://goldrush.dev/guides/introducing-transactions-v3-apis)
[Building Block Explorers (Part 1) - Multi-chain Block Transaction Explorer](https://goldrush.dev/guides/building-block-explorers-part-1-multi-chain-block-transaction-explorer)
[Comparing GoldRush’s Transactions API to RPC Providers](https://goldrush.dev/guides/comparing-covalent-s-transactions-api-to-rpc-providers)
[How to Track Wallets or Transactions with the GoldRush API](https://goldrush.dev/guides/how-to-flag-interesting-wallets-and-or-transactions)
[How to Get the Number of Transactions in a Block](https://goldrush.dev/guides/how-to-get-the-number-of-transactions-in-a-block)
[How to Get All Historical Transactions in a Block](https://goldrush.dev/guides/how-to-get-all-historical-transactions-in-a-block)

#### Authorizations

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-all-transactions-in-a-block#authorization-authorization)

Authorization

string

header

required

Bearer authentication header of the form: `Bearer <token>`, where `<token>` is your GoldRush API Key.

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-all-transactions-in-a-block#parameter-chain-name)

chainName

string

required

The chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-all-transactions-in-a-block#parameter-block-hash)

blockHash

string

required

The requested block hash.

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-all-transactions-in-a-block#parameter-quote-currency)

quote-currency

string

The currency to convert. Supports `USD`, `CAD`, `EUR`, `SGD`, `INR`, `JPY`, `VND`, `CNY`, `KRW`, `RUB`, `TRY`, `NGN`, `ARS`, `AUD`, `CHF`, and `GBP`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-all-transactions-in-a-block#parameter-no-logs)

no-logs

boolean

Omit log events.

#### Response

200 - application/json

Successful response

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-all-transactions-in-a-block#response-updated-at)

updated\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp when the response was generated. Useful to show data staleness to users.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-all-transactions-in-a-block#response-chain-id)

chain\_id

integer

The requested chain ID eg: `1`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-all-transactions-in-a-block#response-chain-name)

chain\_name

string

The requested chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-all-transactions-in-a-block#response-chain-tip-height)

chain\_tip\_height

integer

The latest block height of the blockchain at the time this response was provided.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-all-transactions-in-a-block#response-chain-tip-signed-at)

chain\_tip\_signed\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp of the latest signed block at the time this response was provided.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-all-transactions-in-a-block#response-items)

items

object\[\]

List of response items.

Show child attributes

[Get all transactions in a block by page (v3)](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-all-transactions-in-a-block-by-page)
 [Get NFTs for address](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/nft/get-nfts-for-address)

Credit Cost
-----------

0.01 per item

Processing
----------

Realtime

Related guides

[What are Event Logs?](https://goldrush.dev/guides/evm-event-logs)

#### Authorizations

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-log-events-by-contract-address#authorization-authorization)

Authorization

string

header

required

Bearer authentication header of the form: `Bearer <token>`, where `<token>` is your GoldRush API Key.

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-log-events-by-contract-address#parameter-chain-name)

chainName

string

required

The chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-log-events-by-contract-address#parameter-contract-address)

contractAddress

string

required

The requested contract address. Passing in an `ENS`, `RNS`, `Lens Handle`, or an `Unstoppable Domain` resolves automatically.

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-log-events-by-contract-address#parameter-starting-block)

starting-block

integer

The first block to retrieve log events with. Accepts decimals, hexadecimals, or the strings `earliest` and `latest`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-log-events-by-contract-address#parameter-ending-block)

ending-block

string

The last block to retrieve log events with. Accepts decimals, hexadecimals, or the strings `earliest` and `latest`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-log-events-by-contract-address#parameter-page-size)

page-size

integer

Number of items per page. Omitting this parameter defaults to 100.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-log-events-by-contract-address#parameter-page-number)

page-number

integer

0-indexed page number to begin pagination.

#### Response

200 - application/json

Successful response

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-log-events-by-contract-address#response-updated-at)

updated\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp when the response was generated. Useful to show data staleness to users.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-log-events-by-contract-address#response-chain-id)

chain\_id

integer

The requested chain ID eg: `1`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-log-events-by-contract-address#response-chain-name)

chain\_name

string

The requested chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-log-events-by-contract-address#response-items)

items

object\[\]

List of response items.

Show child attributes

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-log-events-by-contract-address#response-pagination)

pagination

object

Pagination metadata.

Show child attributes

[Get log events by topic hash(es)](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-log-events-by-topic-hash)
[Get a block](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-a-block)

Credit Cost
-----------

0.01 per item

Processing
----------

Realtime

Related guides

[How to Fetch User Operations (UserOps) for a Specific Wallet Address](https://goldrush.dev/guides/how-to-fetch-user-operations-userops-for-a-specific-wallet-address)
[What are Event Logs?](https://goldrush.dev/guides/evm-event-logs)

#### Authorizations

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-log-events-by-topic-hash#authorization-authorization)

Authorization

string

header

required

Bearer authentication header of the form: `Bearer <token>`, where `<token>` is your GoldRush API Key.

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-log-events-by-topic-hash#parameter-chain-name)

chainName

string

required

The chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-log-events-by-topic-hash#parameter-topic-hash)

topicHash

string

required

The endpoint will return event logs that contain this topic hash.

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-log-events-by-topic-hash#parameter-starting-block)

starting-block

integer

The first block to retrieve log events with. Accepts decimals, hexadecimals, or the strings `earliest` and `latest`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-log-events-by-topic-hash#parameter-ending-block)

ending-block

string

The last block to retrieve log events with. Accepts decimals, hexadecimals, or the strings `earliest` and `latest`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-log-events-by-topic-hash#parameter-secondary-topics)

secondary-topics

string

Additional topic hash(es) to filter on - padded & unpadded address fields are supported. Separate multiple topics with a comma.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-log-events-by-topic-hash#parameter-page-size)

page-size

integer

Number of items per page. Omitting this parameter defaults to 100.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-log-events-by-topic-hash#parameter-page-number)

page-number

integer

0-indexed page number to begin pagination.

#### Response

200 - application/json

Successful response

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-log-events-by-topic-hash#response-updated-at)

updated\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp when the response was generated. Useful to show data staleness to users.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-log-events-by-topic-hash#response-chain-id)

chain\_id

integer

The requested chain ID eg: `1`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-log-events-by-topic-hash#response-chain-name)

chain\_name

string

The requested chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-log-events-by-topic-hash#response-chain-tip-height)

chain\_tip\_height

integer

The latest block height of the blockchain at the time this response was provided.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-log-events-by-topic-hash#response-chain-tip-signed-at)

chain\_tip\_signed\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp of the latest signed block at the time this response was provided.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-log-events-by-topic-hash#response-items)

items

object\[\]

List of response items.

Show child attributes

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-log-events-by-topic-hash#response-pagination)

pagination

object

Pagination metadata.

Show child attributes

[Get logs](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-logs)
[Get log events by contract address](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-log-events-by-contract-address)

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/graphql-endpoints#list-of-endpoints)

List of endpoints
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Functionality | Endpoint Type |     |
| --- | --- | --- |
| New DEX Pairs Stream | `subscription` | `subscription { newPairs { ... } }` |
| Wallet ActivityStream | `subscription` | `subscription { walletTxs { ... } }` |
| OHLC Pairs Stream | `subscription` | `subscription { ohlcvCandlesForPair { ... } }` |
| OHLC Tokens Stream | `subscription` | `subscription { ohlcvCandlesForToken { ... } }` |
| Get top trading wallets for token | `query` | `query { upnlForToken { ... } }` |
| Get PnL for wallet | `query` | `query { upnlForWallet { ... } }` |

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/graphql-endpoints#fetching-the-schema)

Fetching the schema
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    query IntrospectionQuery {
      __schema {
        queryType {
          name
        }
        mutationType {
          name
        }
        subscriptionType {
          name
        }
        types {
          ...FullType
        }
        directives {
          name
          description
    
          locations
          args {
            ...InputValue
          }
        }
      }
    }
    
    fragment FullType on __Type {
      kind
      name
      description
    
      fields(includeDeprecated: true) {
        name
        description
        args {
          ...InputValue
        }
        type {
          ...TypeRef
        }
        isDeprecated
        deprecationReason
      }
      inputFields {
        ...InputValue
      }
      interfaces {
        ...TypeRef
      }
      enumValues(includeDeprecated: true) {
        name
        description
        isDeprecated
        deprecationReason
      }
      possibleTypes {
        ...TypeRef
      }
    }
    
    fragment InputValue on __InputValue {
      name
      description
      type {
        ...TypeRef
      }
      defaultValue
    }
    
    fragment TypeRef on __Type {
      kind
      name
      ofType {
        kind
        name
        ofType {
          kind
          name
          ofType {
            kind
            name
            ofType {
              kind
              name
              ofType {
                kind
                name
                ofType {
                  kind
                  name
                  ofType {
                    kind
                    name
                    ofType {
                      kind
                      name
                      ofType {
                        kind
                        name
                      }
                    }
                  }
                }
              }
            }
          }
        }
      }
    }

# Get top trading wallets for token - GoldRush API Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-token#content-area)

[GoldRush API Documentation home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/goldrush/6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA&q=85&s=97917fde1507b0c14e79b83959fe1160)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/goldrush/6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA&q=85&s=5bd4f921dcc81186bf369e7b33ec5734)](https://goldrush.dev/docs)

⌘K

Navigation

Available Queries

Get top trading wallets for token

[Overview](https://goldrush.dev/docs/overview)
[Foundational API](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api/overview)
[Streaming API](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/overview)
[Chains](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/overview)

On this page

*   [Parameters](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-token#parameters)
    
*   [Query](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-token#query)
    
*   [Basic Query](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-token#basic-query)
    
*   [Complete Query](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-token#complete-query)
    
*   [Response Format](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-token#response-format)
    
*   [Field Descriptions](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-token#field-descriptions)
    
*   [GraphQL Playground](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-token#graphql-playground)
    

This GraphQL query provides a list of wallets with the highest trading volume for a specific token over the last 30 days, along with detailed information about their holdings, transaction activity, realized and unrealized profit/loss metrics. This documentation follows our standard streaming API structure.

Credit Cost
-----------

TBD

Supported Chains
----------------

*   Base Mainnet
*   BSC Mainnet
*   Ethereum Mainnet
*   Gnosis Mainnet
*   Polygon Mainnet
*   Optimism Mainnet

**This query is currently in Beta.** It is stable for testing and evaluation but may undergo changes in schema or behavior as we continue to improve it. **No API credits are currently charged.**We welcome your feedback so please [reach out](https://goldrush.dev/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#f685838686998482b6959980979a9398829e87d895999b)
 to us directly to report issues or request features.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-token#parameters)

Parameters
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Required | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `chain_name` | `enum` | Yes | Chain name to filter events (e.g., `BASE_MAINNET`, `ETH_MAINNET`, `BSC_MAINNET`) |
| `token_address` | `string` | Yes | The deployed token contract address to query |

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-token#query)

Query
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can query the `upnlForToken` endpoint to retrieve top wallet trading data.

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-token#basic-query)

Basic Query

Copy

Ask AI

    query {
     upnlForToken(
        chain_name: ETH_MAINNET
        token_address: "0x7ABc8A5768E6bE61A6c693a6e4EAcb5B60602C4D"
      ) {
        token
        address
        volume
        balance
        pnl_realized_usd
        pnl_unrealized_usd
      }
    }
    
    

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-token#complete-query)

Complete Query

Copy

Ask AI

    query {
     upnlForToken(
        chain_name: ETH_MAINNET
        token_address: "0x7ABc8A5768E6bE61A6c693a6e4EAcb5B60602C4D"
      ) {
        token
        address
        volume
        transactions_count
        pnl_realized_usd
        balance
        balance_pretty
        pnl_unrealized_usd
        contract_metadata {
          contract_address
          contract_name
          contract_ticker_symbol
          contract_decimals
        }
      }
    }
    
    

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-token#response-format)

Response Format
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Here’s an example of the response data structure:

Copy

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-token#field-descriptions)

Field Descriptions

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `token` | `string` | Token contract address, represented in lowercase with a 0x prefix |
| `address` | `string` | Wallet address of the token trader, also in lowercase with a 0x prefix |
| `volume` | `BigInteger` | Total volume of tokens transferred by this wallet in the past 30 days |
| `transactions_count` | `integer` | Number of transactions involving this wallet and token in the past 30 days |
| `pnl_realized_usd` | `float` | Realized profit or loss in USD from completed trades |
| `balance` | `BigInteger` | Current token balance in raw format (full decimal precision) |
| `balance_pretty` | `string` | Human-readable token balance formatted to 4 decimal places |
| `pnl_unrealized_usd` | `float` | Unrealized profit or loss in USD based on the current token price |
| `contract_metadata` | `object` | Contains metadata details for the token contract |

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-token#graphql-playground)

[Get PnL for wallet](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-wallet)
