Credit Cost
-----------

0.1 per item

Processing
----------

Realtime

Requests that return status 200 and no data cost 0.1 credits.

Related guides

[What are Deterministic Wallets and How They Work?](https://goldrush.dev/guides/what-are-deterministic-wallets-and-how-they-work)

#### Authorizations

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-bitcoin-balances-for-hd-address#authorization-authorization)

Authorization

string

header

required

Bearer authentication header of the form: `Bearer <token>`, where `<token>` is your GoldRush API Key.

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-bitcoin-balances-for-hd-address#parameter-wallet-address)

walletAddress

string

required

The extended public key (xPub/yPub/zPub) of the HD wallet.

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-bitcoin-balances-for-hd-address#parameter-quote-currency)

quote-currency

string

The currency to convert the balance to. Supports `USD`, `CAD`, `EUR`, etc.

#### Response

200 - application/json

Successful response

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-bitcoin-balances-for-hd-address#response-address)

address

string

The extended public key (xPub/yPub/zPub) or HD wallet address.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-bitcoin-balances-for-hd-address#response-chain-id)

chain\_id

integer

The requested chain ID eg: `20090103`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-bitcoin-balances-for-hd-address#response-chain-name)

chain\_name

string

The requested chain name eg: `btc-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-bitcoin-balances-for-hd-address#response-chain-tip-height)

chain\_tip\_height

integer

The latest block height of the blockchain at the time this response was provided.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-bitcoin-balances-for-hd-address#response-chain-tip-signed-at)

chain\_tip\_signed\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp of the latest signed block at the time this response was provided.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-bitcoin-balances-for-hd-address#response-quote-currency)

quote\_currency

string

The requested quote currency eg: `USD`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-bitcoin-balances-for-hd-address#response-updated-at)

updated\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp when the response was generated. Useful to show data staleness to users.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-bitcoin-balances-for-hd-address#response-items)

items

object\[\]

List of HD wallet balance items, each containing derived addresses and balances.

Show child attributes

[Get token approvals for address](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/security/get-token-approvals-for-address)
[Get Bitcoin balance for non-HD address](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-bitcoin-balance-for-address)

Credit Cost
-----------

0.1 per item

Processing
----------

Realtime

Only supports non-HD bitcoin addresses.

#### Authorizations

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-transactions-for-bitcoin-address#authorization-authorization)

Authorization

string

header

required

Bearer authentication header of the form: `Bearer <token>`, where `<token>` is your GoldRush API Key.

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-transactions-for-bitcoin-address#parameter-address)

address

string

The bitcoin address to query.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-transactions-for-bitcoin-address#parameter-page-size)

page-size

integer

Number of items per page. Omitting this parameter defaults to 100.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-transactions-for-bitcoin-address#parameter-page-number)

page-number

integer

0-indexed page number to begin pagination.

#### Response

200 - application/json

Successful response

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-transactions-for-bitcoin-address#response-updated-at)

updated\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp when the response was generated. Useful to show data staleness to users.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-transactions-for-bitcoin-address#response-items)

items

object\[\]

List of response items.

Show child attributes

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-transactions-for-bitcoin-address#response-pagination)

pagination

object

Pagination metadata.

Show child attributes

Credit Cost
-----------

1 per call

Processing
----------

Realtime

#### Authorizations

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-bitcoin-balance-for-address#authorization-authorization)

Authorization

string

header

required

Bearer authentication header of the form: `Bearer <token>`, where `<token>` is your GoldRush API Key.

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-bitcoin-balance-for-address#parameter-wallet-address)

walletAddress

string

required

Only Bitcoin non-HD addresses are supported.

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-bitcoin-balance-for-address#parameter-quote-currency)

quote-currency

string

The currency to convert. Supports `USD`, `CAD`, `EUR`, `SGD`, `INR`, `JPY`, `VND`, `CNY`, `KRW`, `RUB`, `TRY`, `NGN`, `ARS`, `AUD`, `CHF`, and `GBP`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-bitcoin-balance-for-address#parameter-block-height)

block-height

integer

Ending block to define a block range. Omitting this parameter defaults to the latest block height.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-bitcoin-balance-for-address#parameter-date)

date

string

Ending date to define a block range (YYYY-MM-DD). Omitting this parameter defaults to the current date.

#### Response

200 - application/json

Successful response

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-bitcoin-balance-for-address#response-address)

address

string

The requested address.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-bitcoin-balance-for-address#response-updated-at)

updated\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp when the response was generated. Useful to show data staleness to users.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-bitcoin-balance-for-address#response-quote-currency)

quote\_currency

string

The requested quote currency eg: `USD`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-bitcoin-balance-for-address#response-chain-id)

chain\_id

integer

The requested chain ID eg: `1`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-bitcoin-balance-for-address#response-chain-name)

chain\_name

string

The requested chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-bitcoin-balance-for-address#response-chain-tip-height)

chain\_tip\_height

integer

The latest block height of the blockchain at the time this response was provided.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-bitcoin-balance-for-address#response-chain-tip-signed-at)

chain\_tip\_signed\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp of the latest signed block at the time this response was provided.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-bitcoin-balance-for-address#response-items)

items

object\[\]

List of response items.

Show child attributes

[Get Bitcoin balance for non-HD address](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-bitcoin-balance-for-address)
[Get Bitcoin transactions for non-HD address](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-transactions-for-bitcoin-address)

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/cross-chain/get-address-activity#authorization-authorization)

Authorization

string

header

required

Bearer authentication header of the form: `Bearer <token>`, where `<token>` is your GoldRush API Key.

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/cross-chain/get-address-activity#parameter-wallet-address)

walletAddress

string

required

The requested wallet address. Passing in an `ENS`, `RNS`, `Lens Handle`, or an `Unstoppable Domain` resolves automatically.

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/cross-chain/get-address-activity#parameter-testnets)

testnets

boolean

Set to true to include testnets with activity in the response. By default, it's set to `false` and only returns mainnet activity.

#### Response

200 - application/json

Successful response

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/cross-chain/get-address-activity#response-updated-at)

updated\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp when the response was generated. Useful to show data staleness to users.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/cross-chain/get-address-activity#response-address)

address

string

The requested address.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/cross-chain/get-address-activity#response-items)

items

object\[\]

List of response items.

Show child attributes

[Authentication](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api/authentication)
[Get multichain balances](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/cross-chain/get-allchains-balances)

Credit Cost
-----------

0.25 per item

Processing
----------

Realtime

Base cost is `0.1` credits (e.g. requests that return with status `200` but no items).Calls without logs cost `0.1` credits/item.Calls `with-logs` costs `0.2` credits/item.Calls `with-decoded-logs` costs `0.25` credits/item.The following tracing features each cost `0.05` per transaction that they are available for:

*   `with-internal` - includes internal transfers/transactions.
*   `with-state` - includes all transaction state changes with before and after values.
*   `with-input-data` - includes the transaction’s input data such as the Method ID.

Currently, tracing features are supported on the following chains:

*   `eth-mainnet`

This Multichain & Multiaddress Transactions API is supported across all EVM chains. When no chains are specified, the [Foundational Chains](https://goldrush.dev/chains)
 are passed as default.Domain names (e.g. `demo.eth`) are not supported.

#### Authorizations

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/cross-chain/get-allchains-transactions#authorization-authorization)

Authorization

string

header

required

Bearer authentication header of the form: `Bearer <token>`, where `<token>` is your GoldRush API Key.

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/cross-chain/get-allchains-transactions#parameter-chains)

chains

string

Comma separated list of chain names or IDs to retrieve transactions from. Defaults to all foundational chains.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/cross-chain/get-allchains-transactions#parameter-addresses)

addresses

string

Comma separated list of addresses for which transactions are fetched.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/cross-chain/get-allchains-transactions#parameter-limit)

limit

integer

Number of transactions to return per page, up to the default max of 100 items.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/cross-chain/get-allchains-transactions#parameter-before)

before

string

Pagination cursor pointing to fetch transactions before a certain point.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/cross-chain/get-allchains-transactions#parameter-after)

after

string

Pagination cursor pointing to fetch transactions after a certain point.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/cross-chain/get-allchains-transactions#parameter-with-logs)

with-logs

boolean

Whether to include raw logs in the response.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/cross-chain/get-allchains-transactions#parameter-with-decoded-logs)

with-decoded-logs

boolean

Whether to include decoded logs in the response.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/cross-chain/get-allchains-transactions#parameter-with-internal)

with-internal

boolean

Whether to include internal transfers/transactions.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/cross-chain/get-allchains-transactions#parameter-with-state)

with-state

boolean

Whether to include all transaction state changes with before and after values.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/cross-chain/get-allchains-transactions#parameter-with-input-data)

with-input-data

boolean

Whether to include the transaction's input data such as the Method ID.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/cross-chain/get-allchains-transactions#parameter-quote-currency)

quote-currency

string

The currency to convert. Supports `USD`, `CAD`, `EUR`, `SGD`, `INR`, `JPY`, `VND`, `CNY`, `KRW`, `RUB`, `TRY`, `NGN`, `ARS`, `AUD`, `CHF`, `GBP`, `BTC` and `ETH`.

#### Response

200 - application/json

Successful response

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/cross-chain/get-allchains-transactions#response-updated-at)

updated\_at

string<date-time>

Timestamp for when the data was last updated.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/cross-chain/get-allchains-transactions#response-cursor-before)

cursor\_before

string

Pagination cursor pointing to the previous page.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/cross-chain/get-allchains-transactions#response-cursor-after)

cursor\_after

string

Pagination cursor pointing to the next page.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/cross-chain/get-allchains-transactions#response-quote-currency)

quote\_currency

string

The requested quote currency eg: `USD`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/cross-chain/get-allchains-transactions#response-items)

items

object\[\]

List of transactions returned by the API.

Show child attributes

[Get multichain balances](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/cross-chain/get-allchains-balances)
[Get token balances for address](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-token-balances-for-address)

⌘I

# Get resolved address for registered address - GoldRush API Documentation

    const ApiServices = async () => {
        const client = new GoldRushClient("YOUR_API_KEY");
        const resp = await client.BaseService.getResolvedAddress({chainName: "chainName", walletAddress: "walletAddress"});
        console.log(resp.data);
    };

Credit Cost
-----------

1 per call

Processing
----------

Realtime

Related guides

[How to Resolve a Wallet Address Given an ENS Domain](https://goldrush.dev/guides/how-to-resolve-a-wallet-address-given-an-ens-domain)

#### Authorizations

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-resolved-address-for-registered-address#authorization-authorization)

Authorization

string

header

required

Bearer authentication header of the form: `Bearer <token>`, where `<token>` is your GoldRush API Key.

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-resolved-address-for-registered-address#parameter-chain-name)

chainName

string

required

The chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-resolved-address-for-registered-address#parameter-wallet-address)

walletAddress

string

required

The requested address. Passing in an `ENS`, `RNS`, `Lens Handle`, or an `Unstoppable Domain` resolves automatically.

#### Response

200 - application/json

Successful response

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-resolved-address-for-registered-address#response-updated-at)

updated\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp when the response was generated. Useful to show data staleness to users.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-resolved-address-for-registered-address#response-chain-id)

chain\_id

integer

The requested chain ID eg: `1`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-resolved-address-for-registered-address#response-chain-name)

chain\_name

string

The requested chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-resolved-address-for-registered-address#response-items)

items

object\[\]

List of response items.

Show child attributes

[Get all chain statuses](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-all-chain-statuses)
[Enhanced Bitcoin Support](https://goldrush.dev/docs/resources/enhanced-bitcoin-support)

    import { GoldRushClient } from "@covalenthq/client-sdk";
    
    const ApiServices = async () => {
        const client = new GoldRushClient("YOUR_API_KEY");
        const resp = await client.AllChainsService.getTokenBalances({chainName: "chainName", walletAddress: "walletAddress"});
        console.log(resp.data);
    };

Credit Cost
-----------

2.5 per call

Processing
----------

Realtime

Base cost is `2.5` credits (including requests that return with status `200` but no items) for the first page.Subsequent pages cost `1` credit.All EVM chains are supported. When no chains are specified, the [Foundational Chains](https://goldrush.dev/chains)
 are passed as default.Domain names (e.g. `demo.eth`) are not supported.The UNIX `cutoff-timestamp` retrieves the token balance snapshot from the nearest block before the specified timestamp.Balances presented in descending order of the fiat quote value for most major tokens. Minor tokens may be presented in descending order of their `last_transferred_at` timestamp.

#### Authorizations

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/cross-chain/get-allchains-balances#authorization-authorization)

Authorization

string

header

required

Bearer authentication header of the form: `Bearer <token>`, where `<token>` is your GoldRush API Key.

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/cross-chain/get-allchains-balances#parameter-wallet-address)

walletAddress

string

required

The requested address. Domain names (e.g. `demo.eth`) NOT supported.

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/cross-chain/get-allchains-balances#parameter-chains)

chains

string

Comma separated list of chain names or IDs to retrieve token balances from. Defaults to all foundational chains.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/cross-chain/get-allchains-balances#parameter-limit)

limit

integer

Number of token balances to return per page, up to the default max of 100 items.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/cross-chain/get-allchains-balances#parameter-before)

before

string

Pagination cursor pointing to fetch token balances before a certain point.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/cross-chain/get-allchains-balances#parameter-cutoff-timestamp)

cutoff-timestamp

integer

UNIX timestamp to retrieve the balance snapshot from the nearest block before the specified cutoff time.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/cross-chain/get-allchains-balances#parameter-quote-currency)

quote-currency

string

The currency to convert. Supports `USD`, `CAD`, `EUR`, `SGD`, `INR`, `JPY`, `VND`, `CNY`, `KRW`, `RUB`, `TRY`, `NGN`, `ARS`, `AUD`, `CHF`, `GBP`, `BTC` and `ETH`.

#### Response

200 - application/json

Successful response

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/cross-chain/get-allchains-balances#response-updated-at)

updated\_at

string<date-time>

Timestamp for when the data was last updated.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/cross-chain/get-allchains-balances#response-cursor-before)

cursor\_before

string

Pagination cursor pointing to the previous page.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/cross-chain/get-allchains-balances#response-quote-currency)

quote\_currency

string

The requested quote currency eg: `USD`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/cross-chain/get-allchains-balances#response-items)

items

object\[\]

List of token balances returned by the API.

Show child attributes

[Get multichain & multiaddress transactions](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/cross-chain/get-allchains-transactions)
